üìç Brief summary Conclusion

Specifically, in Guangdong, I have stayed at 115 hotels, including 11 in Foshan prefecture-level city. At present, InterContinental Group has 6,380 hotels around the world, including 420 Crowne Plaza hotels and 123 Crowne Plaza hotels in Greater China. This Litai CP is definitely considered superior. Personally, I feel it is the same as Foshan Marriott and Junyu Wende. Compared with Mu Zhizun, they are on equal footing.
2. Surrounding food, attractions and entertainment: Guicheng Street has a developed economy. Like Wuqing in Tianjin, there is also the town of Florence next to the hotel, which is suitable for buying some top-notch goods (interestingly, there is also a holiday shop next to the one in Tianjin). The hotel is surrounded by Poly Real Estate. As one of the 98 state-owned enterprises, Poly's real estate sector only accounts for a small share of the group's business. Even so, compared with ordinary private companies, it is still a giant, and it has been deeply involved in southern Guangdong. Radiating across the country, you can easily encounter Poly's products in any prosperous place in the 21 prefecture-level cities in Guangdong, with guaranteed quality. The time from the hotel to the airport is: Guangzhou Airport is just over an hour; Shadi Airport is about three quarters of an hour; Gaoming Pearl River Delta Shinkansen Airport is one and a half hours. We look forward to opening the airport as soon as possible. We usually take an MPV from Baiyun T1 to the hotel. There are a lot of Lantu here in Guangdong, and the one-way price is more than 600, which is very cost-effective.

msg:The main purpose of this stay is to get together with old friends who haven't seen for many years. My friend arrived at Guangzhou South Railway Station at noon on Friday, and left from South Railway Station at noon on Saturday. Considering the short stay of my friend and avoiding overwork, I chose the Crowne Plaza Hotel Nanhai not far from South Railway Station. Overall, the whole stay experience was very good and we were not disappointed, especially in terms of catering, there were surprises.

This time I booked a package with a superior twin room including breakfast and evening buffet. The front desk acted quickly during check-in. For the remarks when booking, I hope that high floors can be arranged proactively, and they also help to upgrade to a lake view room. The rooms are bright and spacious. Lake-view rooms on high floors can overlook the lake in the park downstairs, and there are no obvious blocking buildings nearby. The bed in the room is significantly larger than that of the general Crowne Plaza Hotel. It is very friendly for families with children and sleeps comfortably.

The location of the hotel is very good for leisure tourists, about half an hour from Panyu, not far from South Railway Station and Chimelong. There is a park downstairs of the hotel. It may be due to working days. There are not many people. It is refreshing to take a walk with friends before eating. It seems that there are not many businesses within the walking distance. Since the purpose of this trip is to meet with friends, it has little impact on the individual.

Dinner and breakfast are served in the western restaurant on the first floor. The buffet dinner category is similar to other restaurants, including seafood, salmon, grilled oysters and scallops, freshly fried steak, lamb rack and fish, etc. In addition to general fruit juice and soft drinks, there are also boxed Wanglaoji, red and white wine. Although it is a buffet, the chef's intentions are clearly experienced in some details. Some Western-style dishes, such as salted pork knuckle, pork neck, and red wine mutton, have side dishes and meat separately, and the matching is reasonable. Unlike some buffets, the vegetables are soft and yellow, regardless of color and taste, they are satisfactory. In terms of ingredients, I also feel that the hotel has requirements. Even the small blackberries and raspberries decorated on the dessert cakes are very fresh and in good condition. In addition to providing common Chinese and Western dishes, the hotel also adds some local elements to the menu, such as raw porridge and steamed rice rolls. You can also choose pig offal for raw porridge, although pig offal may not be acceptable to everyone (personally is super I like it - but it is also recommended not to have pig lungs, my friend said it is unacceptable), but one of the purposes of tourism is to experience the local culture, so that guests can have the opportunity to experience some local food culture, personally think it is very good. Other food, such as Buddha jumping over the wall for dinner, poplar nectar, tiramisu, carrot cake for breakfast, I personally like it very much. In terms of service, I want to find a quiet place to chat with friends, thank the waiter for reserving a place for us.

In fact, there was a small episode during the check-in process. The temperature of the room was too high and the TV cable was loose, resulting in no signal, but it was resolved quickly after reporting the situation.

In general, the whole check-in experience is still very pleasant. In addition to the surprises in the food and beverage, what impressed me the most is the hotel's emphasis on the guest's check-in experience and its determination to pursue perfect service. The room manager will take the initiative to care about us when dining in the restaurant The situation of check-in, I also received a return visit from the hotel staff after I left the hotel, which was really heartwarming.
